BSNGAL TSAM ZHIG BSGOM PAR GSUNGS PA MA YIN GYI 'DU BYED SDUG
BSNGAL LA DONGS NAS SDUG BSNGAL

BSGOM PAR GSUNGS PA YIN LA ,NGED KYI 'DU BYED KYI SDUG BSNGAL DE
YANG KHYOD 'DOD PA LTAR BDAG RTAG PA LA BRTEN PA MA YIN TE, RANG
RGYU LAS DANG NYON MONGS PA'I RKYEN LAS SKYES PA'I PHYIR, 'ON
KYANG 'DU BYED KYI SDUG BSNGAL

BSGOM BA'I BLO DE NI CHOS CAN, SRID PA LAS DNGOS SU GROL BYED

GSUNGS BA TZAM

RTAG PAR BSGOMS PA DANG, ZAG BCAS

KHO NA MI SKYE, DON DAM PAR RGYU GCIG KHO NA LAS 'BRAS BU DU MA
MI SKYE, DON DAM PAR RGYU DU MA LAS 'BRAS BU GCIG KHO NA MI
SKYE,

GSUM DANG SBYAR TE BSHAD NA, MU DANG PO 'GOG PA NI, MIG DBANG
GIS

MIG DBANG GNYIS PA KHO NA SKYED DAM MIG SHES GCIG BU KHO NA
SKYED, DANG PO LTAR NA 'GRO BA THAMS CAD LONG BAR THAL, MIG
DBANG LAS MIG SHES SKYE MI SRID PA'I PHYIR, GNYIS PA LTAR NA
'ANG 'GRO

PA THAMS CAD LONG BAR THAL, MIG DBANG SKAD CIG GNYIS 'THUD NAS
SKYE MI SRID PA'I PHYIR, MU GNYIS PA 'GOG PA NI, MIG SHES KYI
MYONG BA'I CHA NI DE MA THAG RKYEN GYI LAG RJES DANG, YUL GYI
RNAM PA

PA 'DZIN NUS PA'I CHA NI BDAG RKYEN KYI LAG RJES MA YIN PAR
THAL, DON DAM PAR RGYU GCIG KHO NAS 'BRAS BU DU MA SKYED PA'I
PHYIR,

MU GSUM PA 'GOG PA NI, RGYU DU MAS 'BRAS BU GCIG KHO NA SKYED NA

DANG YUL RIS SU CHAD PA 'DZIN NUS KYI CHA GSUM PO'I NANG NAS
GANG RUNG

'GYUR BAS TSE 'DI'I LHAS BYIN GYI SKYE SHI DANG DE DANG RGYUD
GCIG PA'I SKYE BA DANG RGA SHI GNYIS LA SNGA PHYI YIN MIN DBYE
BAR MI NUS SO, ,ZHES GSUNGS

@116A *, ,PA'I PHYIR, CHOS GNYIS NGO BO GCIG LA LDOG PA THA DAD
DU 'JOG PA NI MING BRNGAS BZHAG TZAM GYI DON LA 'THAD PA MA
GTOGS BTAGS DON BTZAL NAS RNYED PA'I DON LA MI 'THAD PA'I PHYIR
TE,

BRTAG PA MTHA' BZUNG BTAGS DON BTZAL NAS RNYED PA'I DBANG DU
BYED NA, NGO BO GCIG YIN NA LDOG PA GCIG YIN DGOS SHING, LDOG PA
THA DAD YIN NA NGO BO THA DAD DANG 'BREL MED DON GZHAN YIN DGOS

PA'I PHYIR TE, DPER NA DNGOS PO DANG DON BYED NUS PA THA DAD DU
'JOG PA NI DNGOS PO DANG DON BYED NUS PA ZHES PA'I MING THA DAD
TZAM GYIS THA DAD DU 'JOG PA MA GTOGS DON THA DAD DU 'JOG LUGS
MED PA

BZHIN YIN PA'I PHYIR, //DZA// DE PHYIR PHUNG PO LAS GZHAN BDAG

DU SNANG BA'ANG MA YIN

'CHAR TSUL SNA TSOGS ZHIG 'BYUNG BAR BSHAD DO,, MKHAS GRUB RJE'I

TSUL NGES PA'I

DRI MA BKRUS PA'I

CHAB KYIS LHAN SKYES KYI MA RIG PA'I DBANG GIS CHOS RNAMS KYI
YIN LUGS LA RMONGS SHING 'KHRUL BA'I GANG ZAG RGYAL PO DUG CAN
BA'I BU DRUG KHRI'I RGYUD TSOGS DAG PAR GYUR CIG ,RIN CHEN RNAM
BZHI'I KHUR

@198A *, ,LCI ZHING ROL BA'I MTSO CHEN GYI SKA RAGS GA-YO LA,
NYI ZLA'I SGRON ME 'DEGS PA'I LHUN PO JI SRID GNAS PA DE SRID DU
BSTAN BCOS 'DIS KYANG GSAR BSHAD KYI KHUR LCI ZHING GRAGS

SNYAN GYI BA DAN GA-YO LA LEGS BSHAD KYI SGRON ME'I 'OD KYIS SA
GSUM SNANG BAR BYED PAR SHOG ,CHOS KYI DBYINGS GDOD MA NAS RNAM
PAR DAG PA'I GSHIS DANG DKON MCHOG GSUM GYI BYIN

RLABS MI BSLU BA'I MTHUS 'GRO BA MTHA' YAS PA RNAMS SANGS RGYAS
KYI RDZU 'PHRUL BZHIN DU SA BCU LAM LNGA RIM BZHIN MYUR DU BGROD
CING, NYA RGYAS TE YAR TSES BCO LNGA'I ZLA BA LTAR SPANGS RTOGS

KYI YON TAN KUN YONGS SU RDZOGS NAS NYI MA BRGYA LAS KYANG CHES
CHER GSAL BA'I KUN MKHYEN YE SHES MYUR DU THOB PAR SHOG CIG ,CES
PA'O, ,'DIR SMRAS PA, YANG DAG LTAR SNANG 'DOD TSUL

MI 'DRA SNA TSOGS RBA RLABS GYA GYUR GA-YO, ,GNAS TSUL GTING ZAB
DAM GNAG 'THUG POS BLO DMAN SNYING LA 'JIGS PA SKYED, ,RJOD BYED
PHA MTHA' MTHONG BAR DKA' BA'I PHYI NANG GZHUNG LUGS

BA TSVA'I MTSOR, ,YUN RING DUS NAS GAB PAR GYUR BA GRUB MTHA'I
KHYAD PAR YID BZHIN NOR, ,GZHUNG LUGS TI MI'I GRONG DU GNAS BCAS
SHING, ,ZAD MED LEGS BSHAD NOR LA DBANG 'BYOR BA, ,

'JAM DBYANGS DGYES BZHAD LAG 'GRO'I DBANG PO DE, ,MKHYEN RAB
BRTZON PA'I STOBS KYIS LEGS PAR RNYED, ,GUS DANG RTAG SBYOR
BRTZON 'GRUS RLUNG GIS BSKYOD, ,RNAM DPYOD MI DMAN RTA LJANG

@198B SHING RTAS DRANGS, ,GRUB MTHA' RTZA 'GREL RI GLING KUN
GSAL BA'I, ,ZUR MCHAN NYIN BYED DBANG PO DENG 'DIR SHAR, ,PHYOGS
LHUNG TSA BAS GDUNG BA RNAMS LA LEGS BSHAD GANGS KYANG CHAR
'GYUR LA, ,PHRAG DOG

LHAG PAS BTAB PA RNAMS LA PHAN 'DOGS ME YANG GRANG BYED MOD,
,MKHYEN RAB GSHOG ZUNG RGYAS PA'I MKHAS MCHOG ZUR GNAS DANG PA'I
RGYAL PO NYID, ,YANG DAG LTAR SNANG 'O CHU 'DRES PA RNAM DPYOD

MCHU YIS 'BYED PAR MDZOD, ,'DIR 'BAD LEGS BYAS RAB DKAR KOO MU
R'IS, ,'GRO BA KUN GYI MTHAR 'DZIN MUN PA DANG, ,SRID PA'I TSA
GDUNG MA LUS BSAL BYAS TE, ,NGES LEGS KUN DA'I DGA' TSAL RGYAS

GYUR CIG ,RGYAL BSTAN SNYING PO ZHVA SER 'CHANG BA'I BSTAN, ,YUL
PHYOGS GNAS SKABS KUN TU RAB RGYAS SHING, ,DE 'DZIN MKHAS MANG
DGE 'DUN SDE DANG BCAS, ,KHRIMS GTZANG THUGS MTHUN BSHAD SGRUB

'PHEL GYUR CIG ,BDAG KYANG MA 'ONGS TSE RABS THAMS CAD DU, ,MTHO
RIS YON TAN BDUN GYIS RAB MDZES SHING, ,THEG MCHOG DGE BA'I
BSHES KYIS ZIN PA'I MTHUS, ,MA NOR LAM BZANG MYUR DU MTHAR

PHYIN SHOG ,GSER GYI RI BO'I BRTZEGS PA RIM PA BDUN GYIS KUN NAS
YONGS SU BSKOR, ,BSIL DANG 'JAM DANG DRI MAS DBEN PA'I ROL
MTSO'I SMAD GA-YOG MDZES PAR GSOL, ,RIN CHEN RNAM BZHI'I

RDUL BRTZEGS LHUN PO JI SRID GNAS PA DE SRID DU, ,MCHAN 'GREL
'DIS KYANG GNAS SHING 'GRO LA LEGS BSHAD DGA' STON 'GYED GYUR
CIG ,CES GRUB MTHA' CHEN MO'I MCHAN 'GREL DKA' GNAD

@199A *, ,MDUD GROL BLO GSAL GCES NOR ZHES BYA BA 'DI NI, KHAL
KHA KHU RE CHEN MO'I BKRA SHIS CHOS 'PHEL GRVA TSANG GI DKA' RAM
PA'I 'DZIN GRVA NAS DAD BRTZON RNAM DPYOD DANG LDAN PA DGE SLONG
SBYIN PA

LEGS BSHAD KYIS GRUB MTHA' CHEN MO LA MCHAN 'GREL GCIG DGOS ZHES
DNGUL GYI MAndAL KHA BTAGS RNAM DBANG GOS CHEN SER PO YUG CHEN
GYI RTEN DANG BCAS NAN TAN GYIS BSKUL BA'I DON DU, YUL

RTA LA KHUR CHEN MOR DBU BRTZAMS TE, MDO SDE PHAL MO CHE NAS

'PHAGS PA 'JAM DPAL GYI SPRUL BA'I GNAS SU GSAL BAR LUNG BSTAN
PA'I RI BO RTZE LNGA'I DBEN GNAS 'JAM DBYANGS CHOS 'KHOR GLING
DU PHAL CHER GRUB PAR BYAS SHING, BKA' DANG BSTAN BCOS

'GYUR RO 'TSAL BZHUGS PA'I GTZUG LAG KHANG CHEN PO DAM CHOS

@199B NYI MA'I ZHABS RDUL SPYI BOS MCHOD, ,RGYAL BA'I SRAS MCHOG

MCHED ZHABS, ,PHYOGS GLANG CHOS GRAGS LA SOGS 'PHAGS

YUL GYI, ,MKHAS MANG SKAR TSOGS THUB BSTAN NAM MKHA'I RGYAN,

@200A *, ,'O MTSO'I DPAL LA DGAR DRAG NAS, ,RGYAL DANG RGYAL
